     <a id="main-content">
     </a>
     <div class="hidden" data-drupal-messages-fallback="">
     </div>
     <div about="/page/homepage" class="page full clearfix" role="article" typeof="schema:WebPage">
      <span class="hidden" content="Homepage" property="schema:name">
      </span>
      <div class="content">
       <div class="paragraph--html-section paragraph--naming-layer">
        <div class="paragraph--container-layer">
         <section class="homepage-hero" style="background-image: url('/sites/www.sketchup.com/files/molecule_image/SU2021-Web-Home-S1-Desktop-Drupal-NoNoise.jpg');">
          <div class="container-fluid wrap">
           <div class="row">
            <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-8 col-md-6">
             <div class="ter-card box-shadow-3">
              <div class="ter-card__body">
               <div class="paragraph--m-header text-left">
                <h1 class="font-size-lg">
                 Where great ideas get to work
                </h1>
               </div>
               <div class="paragraph--m-text text-left">
                <p>
                 Design delightfully. Collaborate clearly. Build better buildings.
                </p>
               </div>
               <div class="paragraph--m-cta-section text-left">
                <div class="cta-section--upper">
                 <div class="block-display text-left">
                  <a class="ter-button ter-button--primary ter-button--large" href="/try-sketchup">
                   Try SketchUp
                  </a>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="homepage-hero__video-container">
           <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="700px" mozallowfullscreen="" src="https://player.vimeo.com/video/314859584?background=1" webkitallowfullscreen="" width="100%">
           </iframe>
           <!--<video autoplay muted loop class="homepage-hero__video">
			<source src="/sites/www.sketchup.com/files/homepage/Timelapse_VBR_3-4mb.mp4" type="video/mp4">
		</video>-->
          </div>
         </section>
         <section style="background: linear-gradient(0deg, #E2E2E7 0%, #F9F9FB 100%);">
          <div class="js-trigger-lottie pad-top-xxl homepage__section">
           <div class="container-fluid wrap height-100">
            <div class="row reverse between-xs height-100">
             <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-5 justify-content-center d-flex flex-column">
              <div class="d-block icon-home-32px margin-bottom-mini">
               <img alt="" height="32" src="/sites/www.sketchup.com/files/homepage/ico-su-blue-square-32px.svg" width="32"/>
              </div>
              <div class="d-block font-size-md color-brand-1 font-weight-black text-uppercase">
               Create
              </div>
              <h3 class="font-size-lg">
               Visualize your ideas
              </h3>
              <p class="font-size-md color-dark-0 font-weight-light">
